 The two-time champions Chennai Super Kings team defeated hosts Delhi Daredevils by 86 runs in the 24th match of the Indian Premier League (IPL) played at the Ferozeshah Kotla ground on Thursday
 super kings kii yah paanch maichon main teesri jeet he jabaki mejabaan team ko lagaataar chhathi baar haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa he
 The Super Kings had a target of 170 runs in front of Delhi, which proved to be huge for them as all the other leading batsmen remained silent except for Kedar Jadhav (31)
 nateeja hua ki mejabaan team 17
 Only scored 83 runs in 3 overs
 kedaar ke alaava jivan mendis (12) or virendra sahvaag (17) dahaai tak pahunch sake
 Apart from Sehwag, Jeevan and Jadhav, opener David Warner (1), Manpreet Juneja (2), captain Mahela Jayawardene (6), Irfan Pathan (2), Ajit Agarkar (3) and Morne Morkel (2) disappointed
 warner kaa wicket 11 ranon ke kul yoga par gira
 He was bowled by Mohit Sharma
 iske baad 13 ke kul yoga par sharma ne juneja ko pagabaadha out kiya
 Jayawardene was dismissed lbw to Chris Maurice for a total of 30 runs
 iske baad isi yoga par sahvaag ko sharma ne out kiya

 sahvaag ke out hone ke baad jadhav or jivan ne paanchaven wicket ke liye 31 ran jode

 pathan 68, agarkar 73 or morkal 80 ran ke kul yoga par pavilion laute
 Jadhav's wicket fell at a total of 82
 jadhav ne 28 gendon par teen chauke lagaae
 Delhi's innings ended with Umesh Yadav (1) falling for a total of 83 runs
 shahbaaj nadeem do ran par naabad rahe

 albi morkal, dwen braavo or mauris ne bhi ek-ek safalataa hasil kii

 Dhoni and Hussey shared a 74-run partnership from 40 balls for the third wicket
 dhoni ne 23 gendon par paanch chauke or ek chakka lagaaya jabaki pari kii shuruyaat karne aae hasi ne 50 gendon par chah chauke or do chakke lagaae

 ' If you live under stress at your workplace, it may prompt you to eat more at night or eat junk food
 yah sthiti aapaki sehat ke liye ghaatak ho sakati he
 a new research suggests that a good night's sleep can protect you from workplace stress and unhealthy food in the evening
 america main mishigan rajya vishvavidhyalay main manovigyaan kii associat professor or is adhyayan kii sah lekhika chu-siyang chang ne kaha, "hamane paaya he ki jin karmchaariyon kaa kaarysthal kaa din tanavbhara rahata he, ve kaarysthal kii apni nakaaratmak bhaawanaaon ko khaane kii mej par laate hai
 The result is that they eat more food than usual and prefer to consume junk food instead of healthy food
 " The findings of the research are published online in the Journal of Applied Psychology
 iske liye china main 235 karmiyon ke do alag-alag adhyayan hue hai
 One study relates to employees of information technology, who are faced with heavy day-to-day work and who feel they never have enough time in the workplace
 doosraa shodh kol centaron ke karmchaariyon se sambandhit he, jo tarah-tarah ke graahakon se baatcheet karte-karte aksar tanaav main aa jate hai
 Ihao Liu, assistant professor at the University of Illinois in the US and co-author of the research report, stated, "in both cases, stress at the workplace is associated with negative behavior of employees during the job and interest in unhealthy eating in the evenings
 " "periodically taking food serves as an activity to calm and control a person's negative behavior," said Liu, as individuals strive to avoid adverse feelings and prefer to accept the intended feelings
 " Liu said, "second, unhealthy eating may be one of the reasons for low self-confidence
 jab baari kaam ke kaaran tanaavpurn bhavanaaen aati hai, tab vyakti saamaanya rup se apni buddhi or vyavhaaron main prabhavi niyantran nahin rakh pate, joki vyakti ke lakshyon or saamaajik mulyon se jude hote hai
 " chang ne is baat ko rekhaankit kiya ki bharpoor neend lenaa aswasthkar bhojan karne, joki kaarysthal ke tanaav ke kaaran hota he, se bachaane main madad karata he
 It also explains how healthy behavior is linked to this
 tippaniyan He said, "good sleep at night refreshes workers, which helps them cope with stress at the workplace the next day and prevents them from eating unhealthy food
 " (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) shodh kaa nishkarsh jarnal of aplide psychology main online prakashit hua he
 For this, two separate studies of 235 personnel have been conducted in China
 ek adhyayan soochna prodyogiki se sambandh karmchaariyon kaa he, jinka rojaanaa ucchstar ke baari kaam se saamana hota he or jo mahasoos karte hai ki unke paas kaarysthal main kabhi paryaapt samay nahin rahata he
 The second research relates to employees of call centers, who often get tense while interacting with a variety of customers
 america main illinois vishvavidhyalay main assistant professor or shodh report ke sah lekhak ihaao liu ne kaha, "donon hi maamalon main, kaarysthal par tanaav naukari ke dauraan karmchaariyon ke nakaaratmak vyavhaar se judaa hua he or shaam ko aswasthkar bhojan main ruchi se judaa he
 " liu ne kaha, "samay-samay par bhojan lenaa kisi vyakti ke nakaaratmak vyavhaar ko shant or niyantrit karne kii gatividhi ke rup main kaary karata he, kyonki vyakti pratikul bhaawanaaon se bachane kaa prayaas karte hai or icchit bhaawanaaon ko sweekaar karnaa pasand karte hai
 " liu ne kaha, "doosraa, aswasthkar bhojan aatmavishvaas ke kam hone kaa ek kaaran ho saktaa he
 When stressful emotions occur due to heavy work, individuals are generally not able to exercise effective control over their intelligence and behaviors, which are associated with the person's goals and social values
 " Chang underlined that getting plenty of sleep helps prevent unhealthy eating, which is caused by workplace stress
 yah ye bhi bataata he ki kaise isse swasth vyavhaar judaa hua he
 The comments unhone kaha, "raat main acchhee neend karmiyon ko dobaaraa tarotaaja banaati he, jo unhen agle din kaarysthal par tanaav se nipatane main madad karti he or ve aswasthkar bhojan karne se bachaati he
